                  <form>

                     <orth orig="Bu" lang="ar">فَرُقَ</orth>
                  </form>, (S, Mgh, O, Msb,) and in one dial.      
    <form n="infl">       
                     <orth orig="Bi" lang="ar">فَرِقَ</orth>
                  </form>, (Msb, TA,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">فَرْغٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">فُرْقَانٌ</foreign>, (S, O, Msb, K,) the latter of which has a more intensive signification, (TA,) <hi rend="ital">He made a separation,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">a distinction,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">difference,</hi> (Msb, K, TA,) <hi rend="ital">between the two things,</hi> (K, * TA,) or <hi rend="ital">between the parts of the two things:</hi> (Msb:) relating alike to objects of sight and to objects of mental perception: (TA:) IAar, by exs. that he mentions, makes it to relate particularly to objects of the mind, such as sayings; and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n33656-1" target="فرّق" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n33656"/></foreign>, to persons, or material things: (Msb: [and it is stated in the Mgh that the same distinction is mentioned by Az:]) others, however, state that the two verbs are syn.; but that the latter has an intensive signification. (Msb.) It is said in the Kur [v. 28], <foreign lang="ar">فَٱفْرُقْ بَيْنَنَا</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">وَبَيْنَ ٱلْقَوْمِ الفَاسِقِينَ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Therefore decide Thou,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">make Thou a distinction, between us and the unrighteous people</hi>]: accord. to one reading, <foreign lang="ar">فَٱفْرِقْ</foreign>. (Msb, TA.) <foreign lang="ar">فِيهَا يُفْرَقُ كُلُّ أَمْرٍ حَكِيمٍ</foreign>, in the Kur [xliv. 3], means [<hi rend="ital">Wherein</hi>] <hi rend="ital">is made distinct</hi> [<hi rend="ital">every firm decree</hi>]: (Lth, TA:) or <hi rend="ital">is decided;</hi> (O, K, TA;) thus expl. by Katádeh. (O, TA.) And in the phrase <foreign lang="ar">وَقُرآنًا فَرَقْنَاهُ</foreign>, (S, O, K, TA,) in the same [xvii. 107], (S, O, TA,) by <foreign lang="ar">فَرَقْنَاهُ</foreign> is meant <hi rend="ital">We have made it distinct,</hi> (S, O, K, TA,) <hi rend="ital">and rendered it free from defect,</hi> (O, K, TA,) <hi rend="ital">and explained the ordinances therein:</hi> (TA:) but some read   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n33656-2" target="فَرَّقْنَاهُ" n="2" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>, meaning <hi rend="ital">We have sent it down in sundry portions, in a number of days.</hi> (S, TA.) <foreign lang="ar">وَإِذْ فَرَقْنَا بِكُمُ ٱلْبَحْرَ</foreign>, (O, K, TA,) in the Kur [ii. 47], (O, TA,) means <hi rend="ital">And when we clave because of you the sea; i. q.</hi>
